      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Transport">
        Transport
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Transport">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:WroclawDrogi.svg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2386" data-file-width="3138" decoding="async" height="167" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/WroclawDrogi.svg/220px-WroclawDrogi.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/WroclawDrogi.svg/330px-WroclawDrogi.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/WroclawDrogi.svg/440px-WroclawDrogi.svg.png 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:WroclawDrogi.svg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Map of Wrocław illustrating the
         <a href="/wiki/A8_autostrada_(Poland)" title="A8 autostrada (Poland)">
          A8 bypass
         </a>
         and surrounding arterial roads
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Wrocław is a major
       <a href="/wiki/Transport_hub" title="Transport hub">
        transport hub
       </a>
       , situated at the crossroad of many routes linking Western and Central Europe with the rest of Poland.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto2_139-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto2-139">
         [138]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The city is skirted on the south by the
       <a href="/wiki/A4_autostrada_(Poland)" title="A4 autostrada (Poland)">
        A4 highway
       </a>
       , which is part of the
       <a href="/wiki/European_route_E40" title="European route E40">
        European route E40
       </a>
       , extending from the Polish-German to the Polish-Ukrainian border across southern Poland. 
The 672-kilometre highway beginning at
       <a href="/wiki/J%C4%99drzychowice,_Zgorzelec_County" title="Jędrzychowice, Zgorzelec County">
        Jędrzychowice
       </a>
       connects Lower Silesia with
       <a href="/wiki/Opole" title="Opole">
        Opole
       </a>
       and the industrial
       <a href="/wiki/Upper_Silesia" title="Upper Silesia">
        Upper Silesian
       </a>
       metropolis,
       <a href="/wiki/Krak%C3%B3w" title="Kraków">
        Kraków
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Tarn%C3%B3w" title="Tarnów">
        Tarnów
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Rzesz%C3%B3w" title="Rzeszów">
        Rzeszów
       </a>
       . It also provides easy access to German cities such as
       <a href="/wiki/Dresden" title="Dresden">
        Dresden
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Leipzig" title="Leipzig">
        Leipzig
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Magdeburg" title="Magdeburg">
        Magdeburg
       </a>
       and with the
       <a href="/wiki/A18_autostrada_(Poland)" title="A18 autostrada (Poland)">
        A18 highway
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/Berlin" title="Berlin">
        Berlin
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Hamburg" title="Hamburg">
        Hamburg
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto2_139-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto2-139">
         [138]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The toll-free
       <a href="/wiki/A8_autostrada_(Poland)" title="A8 autostrada (Poland)">
        A8 bypass
       </a>
       (Wrocław
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Beltway" title="Beltway">
        ring road
       </a>
       ) around the west and north of the city connects the A4 highway with three major routes –
       <a href="/wiki/Expressway_S5_(Poland)" title="Expressway S5 (Poland)">
        S5 expressway
       </a>
       leading to
       <a href="/wiki/Pozna%C5%84" title="Poznań">
        Poznań
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Bydgoszcz" title="Bydgoszcz">
        Bydgoszcz
       </a>
       ; the
       <a href="/wiki/Expressway_S8_(Poland)" title="Expressway S8 (Poland)">
        S8 express road
       </a>
       towards
       <a href="/wiki/Ole%C5%9Bnica" title="Oleśnica">
        Oleśnica
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA" title="Łódź">
        Łódź
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Warsaw" title="Warsaw">
        Warsaw
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Bia%C5%82ystok" title="Białystok">
        Białystok
       </a>
       ; and the
       <a href="/wiki/National_road_8_(Poland)" title="National road 8 (Poland)">
        National Road 8
       </a>
       to
       <a href="/wiki/Prague" title="Prague">
        Prague
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Brno" title="Brno">
        Brno
       </a>
       and other townships in the
       <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">
        Czech Republic
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Traffic_congestion" title="Traffic congestion">
        Traffic congestion
       </a>
       is a significant issue in Wrocław as in most Polish cities; in early 2020 it was ranked as the fifth-most congested city in Poland, and 41st in the world.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140">
        <a href="#cite_note-140">
         [139]
        </a>
       </sup>
       On average, a car driver in Wrocław annually spends 7 days and 2 hours in a traffic jam.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141">
        <a href="#cite_note-141">
         [140]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <a href="/wiki/Roadblock" title="Roadblock">
        Roadblocks
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Gridlock" title="Gridlock">
        gridlocks
       </a>
       and narrow
       <a href="/wiki/Cobblestone" title="Cobblestone">
        cobblestone
       </a>
       streets around the Old Town are considerable obstacles for drivers. The lack of parking space is also a major setback; private lots or on-street pay bays are the most common means of parking.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142">
        <a href="#cite_note-142">
         [141]
        </a>
       </sup>
       A study in 2019 has revealed that there are approximately 130 vehicles per each parking spot, and the search for an unoccupied bay takes on average 8 minutes.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143">
        <a href="#cite_note-143">
         [142]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Aviation">
        Aviation
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Aviation">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Terminal_T2_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu_(cropped).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="527" data-file-width="1023" decoding="async" height="113" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Terminal_T2_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu_%28cropped%29.jpg/220px-Terminal_T2_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu_%28cropped%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Terminal_T2_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu_%28cropped%29.jpg/330px-Terminal_T2_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Terminal_T2_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu_%28cropped%29.jpg/440px-Terminal_T2_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Terminal_T2_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu_(cropped).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Copernicus_Airport_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Copernicus Airport Wrocław">
          Wrocław Copernicus Airport
         </a>
         in
         <a href="/wiki/Strachowice,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Strachowice, Wrocław">
          Strachowice
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The city is served by
       <a href="/wiki/Copernicus_Airport_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Copernicus Airport Wrocław">
        Copernicus Airport Wrocław
       </a>
       (coded WRO), situated around 10 kilometres southwest from the central precinct. The airport handles passenger flights with
       <a href="/wiki/LOT_Polish_Airlines" title="LOT Polish Airlines">
        LOT Polish Airlines
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ryanair_Sun" title="Ryanair Sun">
        Buzz
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Ryanair" title="Ryanair">
        Ryanair
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Wizz_Air" title="Wizz Air">
        Wizz Air
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Lufthansa" title="Lufthansa">
        Lufthansa
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Eurowings" title="Eurowings">
        Eurowings
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Air_France" title="Air France">
        Air France
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/KLM" title="KLM">
        KLM
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Scandinavian_Airlines" title="Scandinavian Airlines">
        Scandinavian Airlines
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Swiss_International_Air_Lines" title="Swiss International Air Lines">
        Swiss International Air Lines
       </a>
       and air
       <a href="/wiki/Cargo" title="Cargo">
        cargo
       </a>
       connections. In 2019 over a 3.5 million passengers passed through the airport, placing it fifth on the list of busiest airports in Poland.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144">
        <a href="#cite_note-144">
         [143]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145">
        <a href="#cite_note-145">
         [144]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Among the permanent and traditional destinations are
       <a href="/wiki/Warsaw" title="Warsaw">
        Warsaw
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">
        Amsterdam
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/D%C3%BCsseldorf" title="Düsseldorf">
        Düsseldorf
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Frankfurt_am_Main" title="Frankfurt am Main">
        Frankfurt am Main
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Z%C3%BCrich" title="Zürich">
        Zürich
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Budapest" title="Budapest">
        Budapest
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto4_146-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto4-146">
         [145]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <a href="/wiki/Low-cost_carrier" title="Low-cost carrier">
        Low-cost flights
       </a>
       are common among British, Italian, Spanish and Ukrainian travellers, based on the number of destinations.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto4_146-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto4-146">
         [145]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Seasonal charter flights are primarily targeted at Polish holidaymakers travelling to
       <a href="/wiki/Southern_Europe" title="Southern Europe">
        Southern Europe
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/North_Africa" title="North Africa">
        North Africa
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto4_146-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto4-146">
         [145]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Rail_and_bus">
        Rail and bus
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Rail and bus">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Impuls_45WE-024.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2952" data-file-width="5248" decoding="async" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Impuls_45WE-024.jpg/220px-Impuls_45WE-024.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Impuls_45WE-024.jpg/330px-Impuls_45WE-024.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Impuls_45WE-024.jpg/440px-Impuls_45WE-024.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Impuls_45WE-024.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Koleje_Dolno%C5%9Bl%C4%85skie" title="Koleje Dolnośląskie">
          Koleje Dolnośląskie
         </a>
         train at
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Main_Station" title="Wrocław Main Station">
          Wrocław Main Station
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The main rail station is
       <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_G%C5%82%C3%B3wny_railway_station" title="Wrocław Główny railway station">
        Wrocław Główny
       </a>
       , which is the largest railway station in Poland by the number of passengers served (21,2 million passengers a year), and perhaps the most important railroad junction alongside
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Warszawa_Centralna" title="Warszawa Centralna">
        Warsaw Central station
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147">
        <a href="#cite_note-147">
         [146]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The station is supported by
       <a href="/wiki/PKP_Intercity" title="PKP Intercity">
        PKP Intercity
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Polregio" title="Polregio">
        Polregio
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Koleje_Dolno%C5%9Bl%C4%85skie" title="Koleje Dolnośląskie">
        Koleje Dolnośląskie
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Leo_Express" title="Leo Express">
        Leo Express
       </a>
       . There are direct connections to
       <a href="/wiki/Szczecin_G%C5%82%C3%B3wny_railway_station" title="Szczecin Główny railway station">
        Szczecin
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pozna%C5%84_G%C5%82%C3%B3wny" title="Poznań Główny">
        Poznań
       </a>
       , and to Warsaw Central through
       <a href="/wiki/%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA_Fabryczna_railway_station" title="Łódź Fabryczna railway station">
        Łódź Fabryczna station
       </a>
       . There is also a regular connection to
       <a href="/wiki/Berlin_Hauptbahnhof" title="Berlin Hauptbahnhof">
        Berlin Hauptbahnhof
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Wien_Hauptbahnhof" title="Wien Hauptbahnhof">
        Wien Hauptbahnhof
       </a>
       (Vienna), as well as indirect to
       <a href="/wiki/Praha_hlavn%C3%AD_n%C3%A1dra%C5%BE%C3%AD" title="Praha hlavní nádraží">
        Praha hlavní nádraží
       </a>
       (Prague) and
       <a href="/wiki/Budapest_Nyugati_railway_station" title="Budapest Nyugati railway station">
        Budapest-Nyugati
       </a>
       with one transfer depending on the carrier.
      </p>
      <p>
       Adjacent to the railway station, is a central bus station located in the basement of the shopping mall "
       <a href="/wiki/Wroclavia" title="Wroclavia">
        Wroclavia
       </a>
       ", with services offered by
       <a href="/wiki/Przedsi%C4%99biorstwo_Komunikacji_Samochodowej" title="Przedsiębiorstwo Komunikacji Samochodowej">
        PKS
       </a>
       , Neobus,
       <a href="/wiki/Flixbus" title="Flixbus">
        Flixbus
       </a>
       , Sindbad, and others.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148">
        <a href="#cite_note-148">
         [147]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149">
        <a href="#cite_note-149">
         [148]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Public_transport">
        Public transport
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Public transport">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       As of 2020, the public transport in Wrocław comprises 99 bus lines and a well-developed network of 23
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tramways_in_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Tramways in Wrocław">
        tram lines
       </a>
       (with a length over 200 kilometres) operated by the Municipal Transport Company "MPK" (
       <i>
        Miejskie Przedsiębiorstwo Komunikacyjne
       </i>
       ).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150">
        <a href="#cite_note-150">
         [149]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Home_page_151-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Home_page-151">
         [150]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Rides are paid for, tickets can be purchased in kiosks and vending machines, which are located at bus stops, as well as in the vending machines located in the vehicle (payment contactless
       <a href="/wiki/Payment_card" title="Payment card">
        payment card
       </a>
       , the ticket is saved on the card). The tickets are available for purchase in the electronic form via
       <a href="/wiki/Mobile_phone" title="Mobile phone">
        mobile
       </a>
       (
       <a href="/wiki/Mobile_app" title="Mobile app">
        mobile app
       </a>
       :
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MPay" title="MPay">
        mPay
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Apple_Pay" title="Apple Pay">
        Apple Pay
       </a>
       , SkyCash, Mobill,
       <a href="/wiki/Google_Pay" title="Google Pay">
        Google Pay
       </a>
       ). Tickets are one-ride or temporary (0.25h, 0.5h, 1h, 1.5h, 24h, 48h, 72h, 168h).
      </p>
      <p>
       Over a dozen traditional
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Taxicab" title="Taxicab">
        taxicab
       </a>
       firms operate in the city as well as
       <a href="/wiki/Uber" title="Uber">
        Uber
       </a>
       , iTaxi,
       <a href="/wiki/Bolt_(company)" title="Bolt (company)">
        Bolt
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Free_Now_(service)" title="Free Now (service)">
        Free Now
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Other">
        Other
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Other">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nextbike,_6001-Rynek,_Wroc%C5%82aw.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2422" data-file-width="3997" decoding="async" height="133" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Nextbike%2C_6001-Rynek%2C_Wroc%C5%82aw.jpg/220px-Nextbike%2C_6001-Rynek%2C_Wroc%C5%82aw.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Nextbike%2C_6001-Rynek%2C_Wroc%C5%82aw.jpg/330px-Nextbike%2C_6001-Rynek%2C_Wroc%C5%82aw.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Nextbike%2C_6001-Rynek%2C_Wroc%C5%82aw.jpg/440px-Nextbike%2C_6001-Rynek%2C_Wroc%C5%82aw.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Nextbike,_6001-Rynek,_Wroc%C5%82aw.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Wrocław City Bike
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       There are 1200 km of
       <a href="/wiki/Cycling_infrastructure" title="Cycling infrastructure">
        cycling paths
       </a>
       including about 100 km paths on flood embankments. Wrocław has a bike rental network called the City Bike (
       <i>
        Wrocławski Rower Miejski
       </i>
       ). It has 2000 bicycles and 200 self-service stations.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152">
        <a href="#cite_note-152">
         [151]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In addition to regular bicycles, tandem, cargo, electric, folding, tricycles, children's, and handbikes are available, operating every year from 1 March to 30 November. During winter (December – February) 200 bikes are available in the system.
      </p>
      <p>
       Wrocław possesses a
       <a href="/wiki/Scooter-sharing_system" title="Scooter-sharing system">
        scooter-sharing system
       </a>
       of
       <a href="/wiki/Lime_(transportation_company)" title="Lime (transportation company)">
        Lime
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bird_(company)" title="Bird (company)">
        Bird
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Bolt_(company)" title="Bolt (company)">
        Bolt
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Free_Now_(service)" title="Free Now (service)">
        Hive Free Now
       </a>
       –
       <a href="/wiki/Motorized_scooter" title="Motorized scooter">
        motorized scooter
       </a>
       rental is available using a
       <a href="/wiki/Mobile_app" title="Mobile app">
        mobile application
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       Electronic car rental systems include "Traficar", "Panek CarSharing" (hybrid cars),
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153">
        <a href="#cite_note-153">
         [152]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154">
        <a href="#cite_note-154">
         [153]
        </a>
       </sup>
       "GoScooter" and "hop.city" electric
       <a href="/wiki/Scooter_(motorcycle)" title="Scooter (motorcycle)">
        scooters
       </a>
       using the mobile application.
      </p>
      <p>
       A
       <a href="/wiki/Gondola_lift" title="Gondola lift">
        gondola lift
       </a>
       over the
       <a href="/wiki/Oder" title="Oder">
        Oder
       </a>
       called "Polinka" began operation in 2013.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155">
        <a href="#cite_note-155">
         [154]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Wrocław also has a
       <a href="/wiki/Inland_port" title="Inland port">
        river port
       </a>
       on the Oder and several
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Marinas" title="Marinas">
        marinas
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Demographics">
        Demographics
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Demographics">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       See also:
       <a href="/wiki/Demographics_of_Poland#Largest_metropolitan_and_urban_areas" title="Demographics of Poland">
        Urban demographics of Poland
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       In June 2020, the population of Wrocław was estimated at 643,782 individuals,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-population_1-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-population-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       of which 343,036 were women and 300,746 were men.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156">
        <a href="#cite_note-156">
         [155]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Since 2011, the population has been steadily rising, with a 0.142% increase between 2019 and 2020, and a 2.167% increase in the years 2011–2020.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157">
        <a href="#cite_note-157">
         [156]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In 2018, the crude
       <a href="/wiki/Birth_rate" title="Birth rate">
        birth rate
       </a>
       stood at 11.8 and the
       <a href="/wiki/Mortality_rate" title="Mortality rate">
        mortality rate
       </a>
       at 11.1 per 1,000 residents.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto3_158-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto3-158">
         [157]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The median age in 2018 was 43 years.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159">
        <a href="#cite_note-159">
         [158]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The city's population is aging significantly; between 2013 and 2018, the number of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senior_citizen" title="Senior citizen">
        seniors
       </a>
       (per
       <a href="/wiki/Statistics_Poland" title="Statistics Poland">
        Statistics Poland
       </a>
       – men aged 65 or above and women aged 60 or above) surged from 21.5% to 24.2%.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto3_158-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto3-158">
         [157]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Historically, the city's population grew rapidly throughout the 19th and 20th centuries; in the year 1900 approximately 422,709 people were registered as residents and by 1933 the population was already 625,000.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160">
        <a href="#cite_note-160">
         [159]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The strongest growth was recorded from 1900 to 1910, with almost 100,000 new residents within the city limits. Although the city was overwhelmingly
       <a href="/wiki/German_language" title="German language">
        German
       </a>
       -speaking, the ethnic composition based on heritage or place of birth was mixed.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto5_161-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto5-161">
         [160]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162">
        <a href="#cite_note-162">
         [161]
        </a>
       </sup>
       According to a statistical report from 2000, around 43% of all inhabitants in 1910 were born outside
       <a href="/wiki/Silesia" title="Silesia">
        Silesia
       </a>
       and migrated into the city, mostly from the contemporary regions of
       <a href="/wiki/Greater_Poland" title="Greater Poland">
        Greater Poland
       </a>
       (then the
       <a href="/wiki/Prussian_Partition" title="Prussian Partition">
        Prussian Partition
       </a>
       of Poland) or
       <a href="/wiki/Pomerania" title="Pomerania">
        Pomerania
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto5_161-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto5-161">
         [160]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Poles and
       <a href="/wiki/Jews" title="Jews">
        Jews
       </a>
       were among the most prominent active minorities. Simultaneously, the city's territorial expansion and incorporation of surrounding townships further strengthened population growth.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto5_161-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto5-161">
         [160]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Following the end of the Second World War and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Flight_and_expulsion_of_Germans" title="Flight and expulsion of Germans">
        post-1945 expulsions
       </a>
       of the pre-war population, Wrocław became predominantly
       <a href="/wiki/Polish_language" title="Polish language">
        Polish
       </a>
       -speaking. New incomers were primarily resettled from
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eastern_Borderlands" title="Eastern Borderlands">
        areas in the east which Poland lost
       </a>
       (
       <a href="/wiki/Vilnius" title="Vilnius">
        Vilnius
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Lviv" title="Lviv">
        Lviv
       </a>
       ), or from other provinces, notably the regions of Greater Poland,
       <a href="/wiki/Lublin" title="Lublin">
        Lublin
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Bia%C5%82ystok" title="Białystok">
        Białystok
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Rzesz%C3%B3w" title="Rzeszów">
        Rzeszów
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto5_161-3">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto5-161">
         [160]
        </a>
       </sup>
       At the end of 1947, the city's population was estimated at roughly 225,000 individuals, most of whom were migrants.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto5_161-4">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto5-161">
         [160]
        </a>
       </sup>
       German nationals who stayed were either resettled in the late 1940s and 1950s, or assimilated.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163">
        <a href="#cite_note-163">
         [162]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Contemporary Wrocław has one of the highest concentration of foreigners in Poland alongside
       <a href="/wiki/Warsaw" title="Warsaw">
        Warsaw
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Pozna%C5%84" title="Poznań">
        Poznań
       </a>
       ; a significant majority are migrant workers from
       <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">
        Ukraine
       </a>
       ; others came from
       <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">
        Italy
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">
        Spain
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">
        South Korea
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">
        India
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">
        Russia
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">
        Turkey
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164">
        <a href="#cite_note-164">
         [163]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165">
        <a href="#cite_note-165">
         [164]
        </a>
       </sup>
       No exact statistic exists on the number of temporary residents from abroad. Many are students studying at Wrocław's schools and institutions of higher learning.
      </p>
      <div class="timeline-wrapper">
       <map name="timeline_e0ced8b8b88e7ad03be95fcac6cdafd3">
       </map>
       <img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/timeline/e0ced8b8b88e7ad03be95fcac6cdafd3.png" usemap="#timeline_e0ced8b8b88e7ad03be95fcac6cdafd3"/>
      </div>
      <p>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166">
        <a href="#cite_note-166">
         [165]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">
        Religion
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Religion">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       See also:
       <a href="/wiki/Four_Denominations_District" title="Four Denominations District">
        Four Denominations District
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wroclaw_%E2%80%93_Ostrow_Tumski.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1181" data-file-width="1772" decoding="async" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Wroclaw_%E2%80%93_Ostrow_Tumski.jpg/220px-Wroclaw_%E2%80%93_Ostrow_Tumski.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Wroclaw_%E2%80%93_Ostrow_Tumski.jpg/330px-Wroclaw_%E2%80%93_Ostrow_Tumski.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Wroclaw_%E2%80%93_Ostrow_Tumski.jpg/440px-Wroclaw_%E2%80%93_Ostrow_Tumski.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wroclaw_%E2%80%93_Ostrow_Tumski.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Cathedral" title="Wrocław Cathedral">
          Wrocław Cathedral
         </a>
         in the oldest district of
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ostr%C3%B3w_Tumski_in_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Ostrów Tumski in Wrocław">
          Ostrów Tumski
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Wrocław's population is predominantly
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Church" title="Roman Catholic Church">
        Roman Catholic
       </a>
       , like the rest of Poland. The
       <a href="/wiki/Diocese" title="Diocese">
        diocese
       </a>
       was founded in the city as early as 1000, it was one of the first dioceses in the country at that time. Now the city is the seat of a
       <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Wrocław">
        Catholic Archdiocese
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       Prior to
       <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">
        World War II
       </a>
       , Breslau was mostly inhabited by
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Protestants" title="Protestants">
        Protestants
       </a>
       , followed by a large Roman Catholic and a significant Jewish minority. In 1939, of 620,976 inhabitants 368,464 were Protestants (
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Protestants" title="United Protestants">
        United Protestants
       </a>
       ; mostly
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lutherans" title="Lutherans">
        Lutherans
       </a>
       and minority
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Reformed" title="Reformed">
        Reformed
       </a>
       ; in the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prussian_Union_of_churches" title="Prussian Union of churches">
        Evangelical Church of the old-Prussian Union
       </a>
       ), 193,805 Catholics, 2,135 other Christians and 10,659 Jews. Wrocław had the third largest Jewish population of all cities in Germany before the war.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-timesofisraelsynagogue_167-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-timesofisraelsynagogue-167">
         [166]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Its
       <a href="/wiki/White_Stork_Synagogue" title="White Stork Synagogue">
        White Stork Synagogue
       </a>
       was completed in 1840,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-timesofisraelsynagogue_167-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-timesofisraelsynagogue-167">
         [166]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and rededicated in 2010.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-timesofisraelsynagogue_167-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-timesofisraelsynagogue-167">
         [166]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Four years later, in 2014, it celebrated its first ordination of four rabbis and three cantors since the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Holocaust" title="Holocaust">
        Holocaust
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-timesofisraelsynagogue_167-3">
        <a href="#cite_note-timesofisraelsynagogue-167">
         [166]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The Polish authorities together with the German Foreign Minister attended the official ceremony.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-timesofisraelsynagogue_167-4">
        <a href="#cite_note-timesofisraelsynagogue-167">
         [166]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wroclaw_synagoga_Pod_Bialym_Bocianem.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3456" data-file-width="5184" decoding="async" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Wroclaw_synagoga_Pod_Bialym_Bocianem.jpg/220px-Wroclaw_synagoga_Pod_Bialym_Bocianem.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Wroclaw_synagoga_Pod_Bialym_Bocianem.jpg/330px-Wroclaw_synagoga_Pod_Bialym_Bocianem.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Wroclaw_synagoga_Pod_Bialym_Bocianem.jpg/440px-Wroclaw_synagoga_Pod_Bialym_Bocianem.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wroclaw_synagoga_Pod_Bialym_Bocianem.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/White_Stork_Synagogue" title="White Stork Synagogue">
          White Stork Synagogue
         </a>
         , initially opened in 1829
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Post-war resettlements from Poland's ethnically and religiously more diverse former eastern territories (known in Polish as
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Kresy" title="Kresy">
         Kresy
        </a>
       </i>
       ) and the eastern parts of post-1945 Poland (
       <i>
        see
        <a href="/wiki/Operation_Vistula" title="Operation Vistula">
         Operation Vistula
        </a>
       </i>
       ) account for a comparatively large portion of
       <a href="/wiki/Ukrainian_Greek_Catholic_Church" title="Ukrainian Greek Catholic Church">
        Greek Catholics
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Orthodox_Church" title="Eastern Orthodox Church">
        Orthodox
       </a>
       Christians of mostly
       <a href="/wiki/Ukrainians_in_Poland" title="Ukrainians in Poland">
        Ukrainian
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Lemkos" title="Lemkos">
        Lemko
       </a>
       descent. Wrocław is also unique for its "Dzielnica Czterech Świątyń" (Borough of Four Temples) — a part of
       <a href="/wiki/Stare_Miasto,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Stare Miasto, Wrocław">
        Stare Miasto
       </a>
       (Old Town) where a Synagogue, a
       <a href="/wiki/Lutheranism" title="Lutheranism">
        Lutheran Church
       </a>
       , a Roman Catholic church and an Eastern Orthodox church stand near each other. Other Christian denominations present in Wrocław include Adventists, Baptists, Free Christians, Jehovah's Witnesses, Latter-day Saints, Methodists and Pentecostals. There are also minor associations practicing and promoting
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Slavic_neopaganism" title="Slavic neopaganism">
        Rodnovery neopaganism
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168">
        <a href="#cite_note-168">
         [167]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169">
        <a href="#cite_note-169">
         [168]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       In 2007, the Roman Catholic Archbishop of Wrocław established the
       <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20131017014214/http://www.pastoralcentre.pl/" rel="nofollow">
        Pastoral Centre for English Speakers
       </a>
       , which offers Mass on Sundays and Holy Days of Obligation, as well as other sacraments, fellowship, retreats, catechesis and pastoral care for all English-speaking Catholics and non-Catholics interested in the Catholic Church. The Pastoral Centre is under the care of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Conventual_Franciscans" title="Conventual Franciscans">
        Order of Friars Minor, Conventual (Franciscans)
       </a>
       of the
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.zakonfranciszkanow.pl/" rel="nofollow">
        Kraków Province
       </a>
       in the parish of
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ko%C5%9Bci%C3%B3%C5%82_%C5%9Bw._Karola_Boromeusza_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Kościół św. Karola Boromeusza we Wrocławiu">
        St Charles Borromeo (Św Karol Boromeusz)
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170">
        <a href="#cite_note-170">
         [169]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Education">
        Education
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Education">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_universities_and_colleges_in_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="List of universities and colleges in Wrocław">
        List of universities and colleges in Wrocław
       </a>
      </div>

          </div>

      </table>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wroclaw-_Uniwersytet_i_Kosciol_Uniwersytecki.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2790" data-file-width="4454" decoding="async" height="138" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Wroclaw-_Uniwersytet_i_Kosciol_Uniwersytecki.jpg/220px-Wroclaw-_Uniwersytet_i_Kosciol_Uniwersytecki.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Wroclaw-_Uniwersytet_i_Kosciol_Uniwersytecki.jpg/330px-Wroclaw-_Uniwersytet_i_Kosciol_Uniwersytecki.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Wroclaw-_Uniwersytet_i_Kosciol_Uniwersytecki.jpg/440px-Wroclaw-_Uniwersytet_i_Kosciol_Uniwersytecki.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wroclaw-_Uniwersytet_i_Kosciol_Uniwersytecki.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/University_of_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="University of Wrocław">
          University of Wrocław
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wroclaw-_Budynek_Politechniki.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3359" data-file-width="5357" decoding="async" height="138" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Wroclaw-_Budynek_Politechniki.jpg/220px-Wroclaw-_Budynek_Politechniki.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Wroclaw-_Budynek_Politechniki.jpg/330px-Wroclaw-_Budynek_Politechniki.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Wroclaw-_Budynek_Politechniki.jpg/440px-Wroclaw-_Budynek_Politechniki.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wroclaw-_Budynek_Politechniki.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_University_of_Technology" title="Wrocław University of Technology">
          Wrocław University of Technology
         </a>
         – Faculty of Architecture
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Wrocław is the third largest educational centre of Poland, with 135,000 students in 30 colleges which employ some 7,400 staff.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rating_171-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-rating-171">
         [170]
        </a>
       </sup>
       List of ten
       <a href="/wiki/Public_university" title="Public university">
        public colleges and universities
       </a>
       :
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/University_of_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="University of Wrocław">
         Wrocław University
        </a>
        (
        <i>
         Uniwersytet Wrocławski
        </i>
        ):
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172">
         <a href="#cite_note-172">
          [171]
         </a>
        </sup>
        over 47,000 students, ranked fourth among
        <a href="/wiki/Public_university" title="Public university">
         public universities
        </a>
        in Poland by the "Wprost" weekly ranking in 2007
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wprost_173-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-wprost-173">
          [172]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_University_of_Technology" title="Wrocław University of Technology">
         Wrocław University of Technology
        </a>
        (
        <i>
         Politechnika Wrocławska
        </i>
        ):
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174">
         <a href="#cite_note-174">
          [173]
         </a>
        </sup>
        over 40,000 students, the best university of technology in Poland by the "Wprost" weekly ranking in 2007
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wprost6_175-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-wprost6-175">
          [174]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Medical_University" title="Wrocław Medical University">
         Wrocław Medical University
        </a>
        (
        <i>
         Uniwersytet Medyczny we Wrocławiu
        </i>
        )
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-176">
         <a href="#cite_note-176">
          [175]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Akademia_Wychowania_Fizycznego_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Akademia Wychowania Fizycznego we Wrocławiu">
         University School of Physical Education in Wrocław
        </a>
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177">
         <a href="#cite_note-177">
          [176]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_University_of_Economics" title="Wrocław University of Economics">
         Wrocław University of Economics
        </a>
        (
        <i>
         Uniwersytet Ekonomiczny we Wrocławiu
        </i>
        )
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178">
         <a href="#cite_note-178">
          [177]
         </a>
        </sup>
        over 18,000 students, ranked fifth best among public economic universities in Poland by the "
        <a href="/wiki/Wprost" title="Wprost">
         Wprost
        </a>
        " weekly ranking in 2007
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wprost7_179-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-wprost7-179">
          [178]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_University_of_Environmental_and_Life_Sciences" title="Wrocław University of Environmental and Life Sciences">
         Wrocław University of Environmental and Life Sciences
        </a>
        (
        <i>
         Uniwersytet Przyrodniczy we Wrocławiu
        </i>
        ):
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180">
         <a href="#cite_note-180">
          [179]
         </a>
        </sup>
        over 13,000 students, ranked third best among public agricultural universities in Poland by the "Wprost" weekly ranking in 2007
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wprost8_181-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-wprost8-181">
          [180]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Academy_of_Fine_Arts_in_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Academy of Fine Arts in Wrocław">
         Academy of Fine Arts in Wrocław
        </a>
        (
        <i>
         Akademia Sztuk Pięknych we Wrocławiu
        </i>
        ),
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-182">
         <a href="#cite_note-182">
          [181]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Karol_Lipi%C5%84ski_University_of_Music" title="Karol Lipiński University of Music">
         Karol Lipiński University of Music
        </a>
        (
        <i>
         Akademia Muzyczna im. Karola Lipińskiego we Wrocławiu
        </i>
        )
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183">
         <a href="#cite_note-183">
          [182]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ludwik_Solski_Academy_for_the_Dramatic_Arts" title="Ludwik Solski Academy for the Dramatic Arts">
         Ludwik Solski Academy for the Dramatic Arts
        </a>
        , Wrocław Campus (
        <i>
         Państwowa Wyższa Szkoła Teatralna w Krakowie filia we Wrocławiu
        </i>
        )
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-184">
         <a href="#cite_note-184">
          [183]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        The
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tadeusz_Ko%C5%9Bciuszko_Land_Forces_Military_Academy" title="Tadeusz Kościuszko Land Forces Military Academy">
         Tadeusz Kościuszko Land Forces Military Academy
        </a>
        (
        <i>
         Wyższa Szkoła Oficerska Wojsk Lądowych
        </i>
        )
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-185">
         <a href="#cite_note-185">
          [184]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Private universities:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Wyższa Szkoła Bankowa (University of Business in Wrocław )
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/University_of_Social_Sciences_and_Humanities" title="University of Social Sciences and Humanities">
         University of Social Sciences and Humanities
        </a>
        (
        <i>
         SWPS Uniwersytet Humanistycznospołeczny
        </i>
        )
       </li>
       <li>
        University of Law (Wyższa Szkoła Prawa)
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-186">
         <a href="#cite_note-186">
          [185]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        Coventry University Wrocław
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-187">
         <a href="#cite_note-187">
          [186]
         </a>
        </sup>
        (Branch campus of the
        <a href="/wiki/Coventry_University" title="Coventry University">
         Coventry University
        </a>
        , UK)
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Other cultural institutions:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Alliance_fran%C3%A7aise" title="Alliance française">
         Alliance Française
        </a>
        in Wrocław
       </li>
       <li>
        Austrian Institute in Wrocław
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/British_Council" title="British Council">
         British Council
        </a>
        in Wrocław
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="external text" href="http://www.dante.uni.wroc.pl/" rel="nofollow">
         Dante Alighieri Society in Wrocław
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Grotowski_Institute_in_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Grotowski Institute in Wrocław">
         Grotowski Institute in Wrocław
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>

          <div class="thumbimage">
           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ja%C5%9B_i_Ma%C5%82gosia_e83.jpg">
            <img alt="Jaś i Małgosia" data-file-height="3168" data-file-width="4752" decoding="async" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/Ja%C5%9B_i_Ma%C5%82gosia_e83.jpg/220px-Ja%C5%9B_i_Ma%C5%82gosia_e83.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/Ja%C5%9B_i_Ma%C5%82gosia_e83.jpg/330px-Ja%C5%9B_i_Ma%C5%82gosia_e83.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/Ja%C5%9B_i_Ma%C5%82gosia_e83.jpg/440px-Ja%C5%9B_i_Ma%C5%82gosia_e83.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="thumbcaption">
           <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kamienice_Ja%C5%9B_i_Ma%C5%82gosia_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Kamienice Jaś i Małgosia we Wrocławiu">
            Two houses known as
            <i>
             Jaś i Małgosia
            </i>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The Old Town of Wrocław is listed in the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Registry_of_Objects_of_Cultural_Heritage" title="Registry of Objects of Cultural Heritage">
        Registry of Objects of Cultural Heritage
       </a>
       and is, since 1994, on Poland's prestigious list of
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_Historic_Monuments_(Poland)" title="List of Historic Monuments (Poland)">
        National Monuments
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-188">
        <a href="#cite_note-188">
         [187]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Several architectural landmarks and edifices are one of the best examples of
       <a href="/wiki/Brick_Gothic" title="Brick Gothic">
        Brick Gothic
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Baroque_architecture" title="Baroque architecture">
        Baroque
       </a>
       architecture in the country.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-189">
        <a href="#cite_note-189">
         [188]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Fine examples of
       <a href="/wiki/Neoclassical_architecture" title="Neoclassical architecture">
        Neoclassicism
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Gr%C3%BCnderzeit" title="Gründerzeit">
        Gründerzeit
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Historicism" title="Historicism">
        Historicism
       </a>
       are also scattered across the city's central precinct. The
       <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Opera" title="Wrocław Opera">
        Wrocław Opera House
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Monopol_Hotel" title="Monopol Hotel">
        Monopol Hotel
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gmach_Biblioteki_Uniwersytetu_Wroc%C5%82awskiego_przy_ul._Karola_Szajnochy_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Gmach Biblioteki Uniwersytetu Wrocławskiego przy ul. Karola Szajnochy we Wrocławiu">
        University Library
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Ossolineum" title="Ossolineum">
        Ossolineum
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/National_Museum,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="National Museum, Wrocław">
        National Museum
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/Castle" title="Castle">
        castle
       </a>
       -like District Court are among some of the grandest and most recognizable historic structures. There are several examples of
       <a href="/wiki/Art_Nouveau" title="Art Nouveau">
        Art Nouveau
       </a>
       and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Modernist_architecture" title="Modernist architecture">
        Modernism
       </a>
       in pre-war retail establishments such as the
       <a href="/wiki/Barasch_Brothers%27_Department_Store" title="Barasch Brothers' Department Store">
        Barasch-Feniks
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dom_Handlowy_Kameleon" title="pl:Dom Handlowy Kameleon">
        Petersdorff-Kameleon
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Renoma_(Wroc%C5%82aw)" title="Renoma (Wrocław)">
        Renoma
       </a>
       department stores.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-190">
        <a href="#cite_note-190">
         [189]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ostr%C3%B3w_Tumski_in_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Ostrów Tumski in Wrocław">
        Ostrów Tumski
       </a>
       (Cathedral Island) is the oldest section of the city; it was once an isolated islet between the branches of the Oder River. The
       <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Cathedral" title="Wrocław Cathedral">
        Wrocław Cathedral
       </a>
       , one of the tallest churches in Poland, was erected in the mid 10th century and later expanded over the next hundreds of years. The island is also home to five other Christian temples and churches, the
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pa%C5%82ac_arcybiskupi_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Pałac arcybiskupi we Wrocławiu">
        Archbishop's Palace
       </a>
       , the Archdiocese Museum, a 9.5-metre 18th-century monument dedicated to Saint
       <a href="/wiki/John_of_Nepomuk" title="John of Nepomuk">
        John of Nepomuk
       </a>
       , historic tenements and the steel
       <a href="/wiki/Tumski_Bridge" title="Tumski Bridge">
        Tumski Bridge
       </a>
       from 1889.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-191">
        <a href="#cite_note-191">
         [190]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-192">
        <a href="#cite_note-192">
         [191]
        </a>
       </sup>
       A notable attraction are 102 original
       <a href="/wiki/Gas_lighting" title="Gas lighting">
        gas lanterns
       </a>
       which are manually lit each evening by a cloaked
       <a href="/wiki/Lamplighter" title="Lamplighter">
        lamplighter
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-193">
        <a href="#cite_note-193">
         [192]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The early 13th-century Main Market Square (Rynek) is the oldest medieval public square in Poland, and also one of the largest.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto1_194-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto1-194">
         [193]
        </a>
       </sup>
       It features the ornate Gothic
       <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Town_Hall" title="Wrocław Town Hall">
        Old Town Hall
       </a>
       , the oldest of its kind in the country.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto1_194-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto1-194">
         [193]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In the north-west corner of the square is
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Elisabeth%27s_Church,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="St. Elisabeth's Church, Wrocław">
        St. Elisabeth's Church
       </a>
       (Bazylika Św. Elżbiety) with its 91.5-metre-high tower and an observation deck at an altitude of 75 metres. Beneath the basilica are two small medieval houses connected by an arched gate that once led into a
       <a href="/wiki/Churchyard" title="Churchyard">
        churchyard
       </a>
       ; these were reshaped into their current form in the 1700s. Today, the two connected buildings are known to the city's residents as "Jaś i Małgosia", named after the children's fairy tale characters from
       <a href="/wiki/Hansel_and_Gretel" title="Hansel and Gretel">
        Hansel and Gretel
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-195">
        <a href="#cite_note-195">
         [194]
        </a>
       </sup>
       North of the church are so-called "
       <a href="/wiki/Slaughterhouse" title="Slaughterhouse">
        shambles
       </a>
       " (Polish:
       <i>
        jatki
       </i>
       ), a former meat market with a
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pomnik_Pami%C4%99ci_Zwierz%C4%85t_Rze%C5%BAnych" title="pl:Pomnik Pamięci Zwierząt Rzeźnych">
        Monument of Remembrance for Slaughtered Animals
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-196">
        <a href="#cite_note-196">
         [195]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The Salt Square (now a flower market) opened in 1242 is located at the south-western corner of the Market Square – close to the square, between Szewska and Łaciarska streets, is the domeless 13th-century
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Mary_Magdalene_Church_(Wroc%C5%82aw)" title="St. Mary Magdalene Church (Wrocław)">
        St. Mary Magdalene Church
       </a>
       , which during the
       <a href="/wiki/Reformation" title="Reformation">
        Reformation
       </a>
       (1523) was converted into Wrocław's first Protestant temple.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-197">
        <a href="#cite_note-197">
         [196]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cathedral_of_St._Vincent_and_St._James,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Cathedral of St. Vincent and St. James, Wrocław">
        Cathedral of St. Vincent and St. James
       </a>
       and the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Collegiate_Church_of_the_Holy_Cross_and_St._Bartholomew,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Collegiate Church of the Holy Cross and St. Bartholomew, Wrocław">
        Holy Cross and St. Bartholomew's Collegiate Church
       </a>
       are burial sites of
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_Polish_monarchs" title="List of Polish monarchs">
        Polish monarchs
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Henry_II_the_Pious" title="Henry II the Pious">
        Henry II the Pious
       </a>
       and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Henry_IV_Probus" title="Henry IV Probus">
        Henry IV Probus
       </a>
       , respectively.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198">
        <a href="#cite_note-198">
         [197]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The
       <i>
        Pan Tadeusz Museum
       </i>
       , open since May 2016, is located in the "House under the Golden Sun" at 6 Market Square. The manuscript of the national
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Epic_poem" title="Epic poem">
        epos
       </a>
       ,
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Pan_Tadeusz" title="Pan Tadeusz">
         Pan Tadeusz
        </a>
       </i>
       , is housed there as part of the
       <a href="/wiki/Ossolineum" title="Ossolineum">
        Ossolineum National Institute
       </a>
       , with multimedia and interactive educational opportunities.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-199">
        <a href="#cite_note-199">
         [198]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tourism_and_places_of_interest">
        Tourism and places of interest
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Tourism and places of interest">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw%27s_dwarfs" title="Wrocław's dwarfs">
        Wrocław's dwarfs
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wroc%C5%82awska_fontanna_Piotr_Walczak2.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1901" data-file-width="3466" decoding="async" height="121" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Wroc%C5%82awska_fontanna_Piotr_Walczak2.jpg/220px-Wroc%C5%82awska_fontanna_Piotr_Walczak2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Wroc%C5%82awska_fontanna_Piotr_Walczak2.jpg/330px-Wroc%C5%82awska_fontanna_Piotr_Walczak2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Wroc%C5%82awska_fontanna_Piotr_Walczak2.jpg/440px-Wroc%C5%82awska_fontanna_Piotr_Walczak2.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wroc%C5%82awska_fontanna_Piotr_Walczak2.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Fountain" title="Wrocław Fountain">
          Wrocław Multimedia Fountain
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The Tourist Information Centre (
       <a href="/wiki/Polish_language" title="Polish language">
        Polish
       </a>
       :
       <i lang="pl">
        Centrum Informacji Turystycznej
       </i>
       ) is situated on the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Main_Market_Square,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Main Market Square, Wrocław">
        Main Market Square
       </a>
       (Rynek) in building no 14. In 2011, Wrocław was visited by about 3 million tourists, and in 2016 about 5 million.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-200">
        <a href="#cite_note-200">
         [199]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Free
       <a href="/wiki/Hotspot_(Wi-Fi)" title="Hotspot (Wi-Fi)">
        wireless Internet (Wi-Fi)
       </a>
       is available at a number of places around town.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-201">
        <a href="#cite_note-201">
         [200]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Wrocław is a major attraction for both domestic and international tourists. Noteworthy landmarks include the
       <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Fountain" title="Wrocław Fountain">
        Multimedia Fountain
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Szczytnicki_Park" title="Szczytnicki Park">
        Szczytnicki Park
       </a>
       with its
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Japanese_Garden_(Wroc%C5%82aw)" title="Japanese Garden (Wrocław)">
        Japanese Garden
       </a>
       , miniature park and
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_dinosaur_parks" title="List of dinosaur parks">
        dinosaur park
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/University_of_Wroc%C5%82aw_Botanical_Garden" title="University of Wrocław Botanical Garden">
        Botanical Garden
       </a>
       founded in 1811, Poland's largest railway model
       <i>
        Kolejkowo
       </i>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Hydropolis_Centre_for_Ecological_Education" title="Hydropolis Centre for Ecological Education">
        Hydropolis Centre for Ecological Education
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/University_of_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="University of Wrocław">
        University of Wrocław
       </a>
       with Mathematical Tower,
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ko%C5%9Bci%C3%B3%C5%82_Imienia_Jezus_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Kościół Imienia Jezus we Wrocławiu">
        Church of the Name of Jesus
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_water_tower" title="Wrocław water tower">
        Wrocław water tower
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Royal_Palace,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Royal Palace, Wrocław">
        the Royal Palace
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Ropes_course" title="Ropes course">
        ropes course
       </a>
       on the Opatowicka Island,
       <a href="/wiki/White_Stork_Synagogue" title="White Stork Synagogue">
        White Stork Synagogue
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/Old_Jewish_Cemetery,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Old Jewish Cemetery, Wrocław">
        Old Jewish Cemetery
       </a>
       and the
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cmentarz_%C5%BBo%C5%82nierzy_W%C5%82oskich" title="pl:Cmentarz Żołnierzy Włoskich">
        Cemetery of Italian Soldiers
       </a>
       . An interesting way to explore the city is seeking out
       <i>
        Wrocław's dwarfs
       </i>
       – over 600 small bronze
       <a href="/wiki/Homunculus" title="Homunculus">
        figurines
       </a>
       can be found across the city, on pavements, walls and lampposts. They first appeared in 2005.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-202">
        <a href="#cite_note-202">
         [201]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Zoo" title="Wrocław Zoo">
        Wrocław Zoo
       </a>
       is home to the
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Africarium" title="Africarium">
         Africarium
        </a>
       </i>
       – the only space devoted solely to exhibiting the
       <a href="/wiki/Fauna_of_Africa" title="Fauna of Africa">
        fauna of Africa
       </a>
       with an
       <a href="/wiki/Oceanarium" title="Oceanarium">
        oceanarium
       </a>
       . It is the oldest
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_zoos_by_country" title="List of zoos by country">
        zoological garden
       </a>
       in Poland established in 1865. It is also the third-largest zoo in the world in terms of the number of animal
       <a href="/wiki/Species" title="Species">
        species
       </a>
       on display.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-203">
        <a href="#cite_note-203">
         [202]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Small passenger vessels on the
       <a href="/wiki/Oder" title="Oder">
        Oder
       </a>
       offer river tours, as do historic
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tramways_in_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Tramways in Wrocław">
        trams
       </a>
       or the converted open-topped historic buses
       <a href="/wiki/Jelcz" title="Jelcz">
        Jelcz
       </a>
       043.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-204">
        <a href="#cite_note-204">
         [203]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hala_Stulecia_(Wroc%C5%82aw)" title="Hala Stulecia (Wrocław)">
        Centennial Hall
       </a>
       (Hala Stulecia,
       <a href="/wiki/German_language" title="German language">
        German
       </a>
       :
       <i lang="de">
        Jahrhunderthalle
       </i>
       ), designed by
       <a href="/wiki/Max_Berg" title="Max Berg">
        Max Berg
       </a>
       in 1911–1913, is a
       <a href="/wiki/World_Heritage_Site" title="World Heritage Site">
        World Heritage Site
       </a>
       listed by
       <a href="/wiki/UNESCO" title="UNESCO">
        UNESCO
       </a>
       in 2006.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-205">
        <a href="#cite_note-205">
         [204]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1021810730">
       @media all and (max-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery{width:100%!important}}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery{display:table}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery-default{background:transparent;margin-top:0.3em}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery-center{margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery-left{float:left}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery-right{float:right}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery-none{float:none}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery-collapsible{width:100%}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery .title,.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery .main,.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery .footer{display:table-row}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery .title>div{display:table-cell;padding:0.2em 0 0.6em 1.6em;text-align:center;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery .main>div{display:table-cell}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery .gallery{line-height:1.35em}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery .footer>div{display:table-cell;padding:0.2em 0 0.6em 1.6em;text-align:right;font-size:80%;line-height:1em}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery .title>div *,.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery .footer>div *{overflow:visible}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery .gallerybox img{background:none!important}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery .bordered-images .thumb img{border:solid #eaecf0 1px}.mw-parser-output .mod-gallery .whitebg .thumb{background:#fff!important}
      </style>
      <div class="mod-gallery mod-gallery-default mod-gallery-center">
       <div class="title">
        <div>
         Key places of interest
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="main">
        <div>
         <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional nochecker bordered-images whitebg">
          <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 215px">
           <div style="width: 215px">
            <div class="thumb" style="width: 210px;">
             <div style="margin:28px auto;">
              <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mercado_de_Navidad,_Plaza_del_Mercado,_Breslavia,_Polonia,_2017-12-20,_DD_41-49_HDR_PAN.jpg">
               <img alt="" data-file-height="6464" data-file-width="8106" decoding="async" height="144" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Mercado_de_Navidad%2C_Plaza_del_Mercado%2C_Breslavia%2C_Polonia%2C_2017-12-20%2C_DD_41-49_HDR_PAN.jpg/180px-Mercado_de_Navidad%2C_Plaza_del_Mercado%2C_Breslavia%2C_Polonia%2C_2017-12-20%2C_DD_41-49_HDR_PAN.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Mercado_de_Navidad%2C_Plaza_del_Mercado%2C_Breslavia%2C_Polonia%2C_2017-12-20%2C_DD_41-49_HDR_PAN.jpg/270px-Mercado_de_Navidad%2C_Plaza_del_Mercado%2C_Breslavia%2C_Polonia%2C_2017-12-20%2C_DD_41-49_HDR_PAN.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Mercado_de_Navidad%2C_Plaza_del_Mercado%2C_Breslavia%2C_Polonia%2C_2017-12-20%2C_DD_41-49_HDR_PAN.jpg/360px-Mercado_de_Navidad%2C_Plaza_del_Mercado%2C_Breslavia%2C_Polonia%2C_2017-12-20%2C_DD_41-49_HDR_PAN.jpg 2x" width="180"/>
              </a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="gallerytext">
             <p>
              <a href="/wiki/Market_Square,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Market Square, Wrocław">
               Market Square
              </a>
              during Christmas
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </li>
          <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 215px">
           <div style="width: 215px">
