      </div>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Entertainment">
        Entertainment
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Entertainment">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:192px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:2010_Schweidnitzer_Keller.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3592" data-file-width="2730" decoding="async" height="250" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/2010_Schweidnitzer_Keller.jpg/190px-2010_Schweidnitzer_Keller.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/2010_Schweidnitzer_Keller.jpg/285px-2010_Schweidnitzer_Keller.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/2010_Schweidnitzer_Keller.jpg/380px-2010_Schweidnitzer_Keller.jpg 2x" width="190"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:2010_Schweidnitzer_Keller.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Piwnica_%C5%9Awidnicka" title="Piwnica Świdnicka">
          Świdnica Cellar
         </a>
         (
         <i>
          Piwnica Świdnicka
         </i>
         ), one of the oldest restaurant establishments in Europe.
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-krn_206-0">
          <a href="#cite_note-krn-206">
           [205]
          </a>
         </sup>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The city is well known for its large number of
       <a href="/wiki/Nightclub" title="Nightclub">
        nightclubs
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Pub" title="Pub">
        pubs
       </a>
       . Many are in or near the
       <a href="/wiki/Market_Square,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Market Square, Wrocław">
        Market Square
       </a>
       , and in the Niepolda passage, the
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Estakada_kolejowa_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Estakada kolejowa we Wrocławiu">
        railway wharf
       </a>
       on the Bogusławskiego street. The basement of the
       <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Town_Hall" title="Wrocław Town Hall">
        old City Hall
       </a>
       houses one of the oldest restaurants in Europe—
       <a href="/wiki/Piwnica_%C5%9Awidnicka" title="Piwnica Świdnicka">
        Piwnica Świdnicka
       </a>
       (operating since around 1273),
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-krn_206-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-krn-206">
         [205]
        </a>
       </sup>
       while the basement of the new City Hall contains the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Microbrewery" title="Microbrewery">
        brewpub
       </a>
       <i>
        Spiż
       </i>
       . There are many other craft breweries in Wrocław: three brewpubs – Browar Stu Mostów, Browar Staromiejski Złoty Pies, Browar Rodzinny Prost; two
       <a href="/wiki/Craft_brewery_and_microbrewery" title="Craft brewery and microbrewery">
        microbrewery
       </a>
       – Profesja and Warsztat Piwowarski; and seven contract breweries – Doctor Brew, Genius Loci, Solipiwko, Pol A Czech, Baba Jaga, wBrew and Wielka Wyspa. Every year on the second weekend of June the
       <a href="/wiki/Festival_of_Good_Beer" title="Festival of Good Beer">
        Festival of Good Beer
       </a>
       takes place.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto6_207-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto6-207">
         [206]
        </a>
       </sup>
       It is the biggest beer festival in Poland.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto6_207-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-auto6-207">
         [206]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Each year in November and December the
       <a href="/wiki/Christmas_market" title="Christmas market">
        Christmas market
       </a>
       is held at the Main Market Square.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-208">
        <a href="#cite_note-208">
         [207]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Museums">
        Museums
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Museums">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <p>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/National_Museum,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="National Museum, Wrocław">
        National Museum
       </a>
       at Powstańców Warszawy Square, one of Poland's main branches of
       <a href="/wiki/National_Museum_of_Poland" title="National Museum of Poland">
        the National Museum
       </a>
       system, holds one of the largest collections of contemporary art in the country.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mnwr_209-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-mnwr-209">
         [208]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wroc%C5%82aw,_Wn%C4%99trza_-_fotopolska.eu_(178575).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="798" data-file-width="1209" decoding="async" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/Wroc%C5%82aw%2C_Wn%C4%99trza_-_fotopolska.eu_%28178575%29.jpg/220px-Wroc%C5%82aw%2C_Wn%C4%99trza_-_fotopolska.eu_%28178575%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/Wroc%C5%82aw%2C_Wn%C4%99trza_-_fotopolska.eu_%28178575%29.jpg/330px-Wroc%C5%82aw%2C_Wn%C4%99trza_-_fotopolska.eu_%28178575%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/Wroc%C5%82aw%2C_Wn%C4%99trza_-_fotopolska.eu_%28178575%29.jpg/440px-Wroc%C5%82aw%2C_Wn%C4%99trza_-_fotopolska.eu_%28178575%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wroc%C5%82aw,_Wn%C4%99trza_-_fotopolska.eu_(178575).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Interior of the
         <a href="/wiki/National_Museum,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="National Museum, Wrocław">
          National Museum
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Ossolineum" title="Ossolineum">
        Ossolineum
       </a>
       is a National Institute and Library incorporating the
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muzeum_Ksi%C4%85%C5%BC%C4%85t_Lubomirskich_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Muzeum Książąt Lubomirskich we Wrocławiu">
        Lubomirski Museum (pl)
       </a>
       , partially salvaged from the formerly Polish city of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lw%C3%B3w" title="Lwów">
        Lwów
       </a>
       (now Lviv in
       <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">
        Ukraine
       </a>
       ), containing items of international and national significance. It has a history of major World War II theft of collections after the invasion and takeover of Lwów by
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Third_Reich" title="Third Reich">
        Nazi Germany
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">
        Soviet Union
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       Major museums also include the
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muzeum_Miejskie_Wroc%C5%82awia" title="pl:Muzeum Miejskie Wrocławia">
        City Museum of Wrocław (pl)
       </a>
       , Museum of Bourgeois Art in the
       <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Town_Hall" title="Wrocław Town Hall">
        Old Town Hall
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Museum_of_Architecture,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Museum of Architecture, Wrocław">
        Museum of Architecture
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muzeum_Archeologiczne_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Muzeum Archeologiczne we Wrocławiu">
        Archaeological Museum (pl)
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Museum_of_Natural_History_at_University_of_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Museum of Natural History at University of Wrocław">
        Museum of Natural History at University of Wrocław
       </a>
       , Museum of Contemporary Art in Wrocław,
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muzeum_Archidiecezjalne_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Muzeum Archidiecezjalne we Wrocławiu">
        Archdiocese Museum (pl)
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Galeria_Awangarda" title="Galeria Awangarda">
        Galeria Awangarda
       </a>
       , the
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arsena%C5%82_Miejski_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Arsenał Miejski we Wrocławiu">
        Arsenal
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muzeum_Farmacji_Uniwersytetu_Medycznego_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Muzeum Farmacji Uniwersytetu Medycznego we Wrocławiu">
        Museum of Pharmacy (pl)
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muzeum_Poczty_i_Telekomunikacji_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Muzeum Poczty i Telekomunikacji we Wrocławiu">
        Post and Telecommunications Museum (pl)
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muzeum_Geologiczne_im._Henryka_Teisseyre_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Muzeum Geologiczne im. Henryka Teisseyre we Wrocławiu">
        Geological Museum (pl)
       </a>
       , the
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muzeum_Mineralogiczne_im._Kazimierza_Ma%C5%9Blankiewicza_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Muzeum Mineralogiczne im. Kazimierza Maślankiewicza we Wrocławiu">
        Mineralogical Museum (pl)
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muzeum_Etnograficzne_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu" title="pl:Muzeum Etnograficzne we Wrocławiu">
        Ethnographic Museum (pl)
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span id="Wroc.C5.82aw_in_literature">
       </span>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Wrocław_in_literature">
        Wrocław in literature
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Wrocław in literature">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r978413945/mw-parser-output/.tmulti" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
      <div class="thumb tmulti tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:212px;max-width:212px">
        <div class="trow">
         <div class="tsingle" style="width:108px;max-width:108px">
          <div class="thumbimage" style="height:138px;overflow:hidden">
           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Max_Liebermann_-_Portr%C3%A4t_des_Dichters_Gerhart_Hauptmann.jpg">
            <img alt="" data-file-height="1363" data-file-width="1047" decoding="async" height="138" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Max_Liebermann_-_Portr%C3%A4t_des_Dichters_Gerhart_Hauptmann.jpg/106px-Max_Liebermann_-_Portr%C3%A4t_des_Dichters_Gerhart_Hauptmann.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Max_Liebermann_-_Portr%C3%A4t_des_Dichters_Gerhart_Hauptmann.jpg/159px-Max_Liebermann_-_Portr%C3%A4t_des_Dichters_Gerhart_Hauptmann.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Max_Liebermann_-_Portr%C3%A4t_des_Dichters_Gerhart_Hauptmann.jpg/212px-Max_Liebermann_-_Portr%C3%A4t_des_Dichters_Gerhart_Hauptmann.jpg 2x" width="106"/>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="tsingle" style="width:100px;max-width:100px">
          <div class="thumbimage" style="height:138px;overflow:hidden">
           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Theodor_mommsen_2_zangala-ka-WP.jpg">
            <img alt="" data-file-height="550" data-file-width="388" decoding="async" height="139" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Theodor_mommsen_2_zangala-ka-WP.jpg/98px-Theodor_mommsen_2_zangala-ka-WP.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Theodor_mommsen_2_zangala-ka-WP.jpg/147px-Theodor_mommsen_2_zangala-ka-WP.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Theodor_mommsen_2_zangala-ka-WP.jpg/196px-Theodor_mommsen_2_zangala-ka-WP.jpg 2x" width="98"/>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="trow">
         <div class="tsingle" style="width:106px;max-width:106px">
          <div class="thumbimage" style="height:155px;overflow:hidden">
           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Olga_Tokarczuk-9730.jpg">
            <img alt="" data-file-height="1500" data-file-width="1000" decoding="async" height="156" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Olga_Tokarczuk-9730.jpg/104px-Olga_Tokarczuk-9730.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Olga_Tokarczuk-9730.jpg/156px-Olga_Tokarczuk-9730.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Olga_Tokarczuk-9730.jpg/208px-Olga_Tokarczuk-9730.jpg 2x" width="104"/>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="tsingle" style="width:102px;max-width:102px">
          <div class="thumbimage" style="height:155px;overflow:hidden">
           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:RK1906_MG_5104_Marek_Krajewski_(cropped).jpg">
            <img alt="" data-file-height="1248" data-file-width="802" decoding="async" height="156" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/RK1906_MG_5104_Marek_Krajewski_%28cropped%29.jpg/100px-RK1906_MG_5104_Marek_Krajewski_%28cropped%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/RK1906_MG_5104_Marek_Krajewski_%28cropped%29.jpg/150px-RK1906_MG_5104_Marek_Krajewski_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/RK1906_MG_5104_Marek_Krajewski_%28cropped%29.jpg/200px-RK1906_MG_5104_Marek_Krajewski_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" width="100"/>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="trow" style="display:flex">
         <div class="thumbcaption">
          Prominent writers from Wrocław, clockwise from upper left:
          <a href="/wiki/Gerhart_Hauptmann" title="Gerhart Hauptmann">
           Hauptmann
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Theodor_Mommsen" title="Theodor Mommsen">
           Mommsen
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Olga_Tokarczuk" title="Olga Tokarczuk">
           Tokarczuk
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Marek_Krajewski" title="Marek Krajewski">
           Krajewski
          </a>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The history of Wrocław is described in minute detail in the monograph
       <a href="/wiki/Microcosm:_Portrait_of_a_Central_European_City" title="Microcosm: Portrait of a Central European City">
        Microcosm: Portrait of a Central European City
       </a>
       by
       <a href="/wiki/Norman_Davies" title="Norman Davies">
        Norman Davies
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Roger_Moorhouse" title="Roger Moorhouse">
        Roger Moorhouse
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-210">
        <a href="#cite_note-210">
         [209]
        </a>
       </sup>
       A number of books have been written about Wrocław following World War II.
      </p>
      <p>
       Wrocław philologist and writer
       <a href="/wiki/Marek_Krajewski" title="Marek Krajewski">
        Marek Krajewski
       </a>
       wrote a series of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Crime_novel" title="Crime novel">
        crime novels
       </a>
       about detective
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eberhard_Mock" title="Eberhard Mock">
        Eberhard Mock
       </a>
       , a fictional character from the city of Breslau.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-211">
        <a href="#cite_note-211">
         [210]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Accordingly, Michał Kaczmarek published
       <i>
        Wrocław according to Eberhard Mock – Guide based on the books by Marek Krajewski
       </i>
       . In 2011 appeared the 1104-page Lexicon of the architecture of Wrocław and in 2013 a 960-page Lexicon about the greenery of Wrocław. In March 2015 Wrocław filed an application to become a
       <a href="/wiki/UNESCO" title="UNESCO">
        UNESCO
       </a>
       's
       <a href="/wiki/City_of_Literature" title="City of Literature">
        City of Literature
       </a>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-212">
        <a href="#cite_note-212">
         [211]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and received it in 2019.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span id="Films.2C_music_and_theatre">
       </span>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Films,_music_and_theatre">
        Films, music and theatre
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Films, music and theatre">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Wrocław is home to the Audiovisual Technology Center (formerly Wytwórnia Filmów Fabularnych), the Film Stuntman School, ATM Grupa, Grupa 13, and Tako Media.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-213">
        <a href="#cite_note-213">
         [212]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Film directors
       <a href="/wiki/Andrzej_Wajda" title="Andrzej Wajda">
        Andrzej Wajda
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Krzysztof_Kie%C5%9Blowski" title="Krzysztof Kieślowski">
        Krzysztof Kieślowski
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Sylwester_Ch%C4%99ci%C5%84ski" title="Sylwester Chęciński">
        Sylwester Chęciński
       </a>
       , among others, made their film debuts in Wrocław. Numerous movies shot around the city include
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Ashes_and_Diamonds" title="Ashes and Diamonds">
         Ashes and Diamonds
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/The_Saragossa_Manuscript_(film)" title="The Saragossa Manuscript (film)">
         The Saragossa Manuscript
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Sami_swoi" title="Sami swoi">
         Sami swoi
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/The_Doll_(1968_film)" title="The Doll (1968 film)">
         Lalka
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/A_Lonely_Woman" title="A Lonely Woman">
         A Lonely Woman
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Character_(film)" title="Character (film)">
         Character
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Aim%C3%A9e_%26_Jaguar" title="Aimée &amp; Jaguar">
         Aimée &amp; Jaguar
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Avalon_(2001_film)" title="Avalon (2001 film)">
         Avalon
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/A_Woman_in_Berlin_(film)" title="A Woman in Berlin (film)">
         A Woman in Berlin
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Suicide_Room" title="Suicide Room">
         Suicide Room
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/The_Winner_(2011_film)" title="The Winner (2011 film)">
         The Winner
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/80_Million" title="80 Million">
         80 Million
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Run_Boy_Run_(film)" title="Run Boy Run (film)">
         Run Boy Run
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Bridge_of_Spies_(film)" title="Bridge of Spies (film)">
         Bridge of Spies
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Breaking_the_Limits" title="Breaking the Limits">
         Breaking the Limits
        </a>
       </i>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-214">
        <a href="#cite_note-214">
         [213]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Narodowe_Forum_Muzyki_im._Witolda_Lutos%C5%82awskiego_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1280" data-file-width="1920" decoding="async" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Narodowe_Forum_Muzyki_im._Witolda_Lutos%C5%82awskiego_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu.jpg/220px-Narodowe_Forum_Muzyki_im._Witolda_Lutos%C5%82awskiego_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Narodowe_Forum_Muzyki_im._Witolda_Lutos%C5%82awskiego_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu.jpg/330px-Narodowe_Forum_Muzyki_im._Witolda_Lutos%C5%82awskiego_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Narodowe_Forum_Muzyki_im._Witolda_Lutos%C5%82awskiego_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu.jpg/440px-Narodowe_Forum_Muzyki_im._Witolda_Lutos%C5%82awskiego_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Narodowe_Forum_Muzyki_im._Witolda_Lutos%C5%82awskiego_we_Wroc%C5%82awiu.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/National_Forum_of_Music" title="National Forum of Music">
          National Forum of Music
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Numerous Polish TV-series were also shot in Wrocław, notably
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/%C5%9Awiat_wed%C5%82ug_Kiepskich" title="Świat według Kiepskich">
         Świat według Kiepskich
        </a>
       </i>
       ,
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Pierwsza_mi%C5%82o%C5%9B%C4%87" title="Pierwsza miłość">
         Pierwsza miłość
        </a>
       </i>
       ,
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Belfer_(TV_series)" title="Belfer (TV series)">
         Belfer
        </a>
       </i>
       , and
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Four_Tank-Men_and_a_Dog" title="Four Tank-Men and a Dog">
         Four Tank-Men and a Dog
        </a>
       </i>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       There are several theatres and theatre groups, including
       <a href="/wiki/Polish_Theatre_in_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Polish Theatre in Wrocław">
        Polish Theatre
       </a>
       (Teatr Polski) with three stages, and Contemporary Theatre (Wrocławski Teatr Współczesny). The International Theatre Festival Dialog-Wrocław is held every 2 years.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-215">
        <a href="#cite_note-215">
         [214]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Wrocław's opera traditions are dating back to the first half of the seventeenth century and sustained by the
       <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Opera" title="Wrocław Opera">
        Wrocław Opera
       </a>
       , built between 1839 and 1841. Wrocław Philharmonic, established in 1954 by Wojciech Dzieduszycki is also important for music lovers. The
       <a href="/wiki/National_Forum_of_Music" title="National Forum of Music">
        National Forum of Music
       </a>
       was opened in 2015 and is a famous landmark, designed by the Polish architectural firm,
       <a href="/wiki/Stefan_Kury%C5%82owicz" title="Stefan Kuryłowicz">
        Kurylowicz &amp; Associates
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-216">
        <a href="#cite_note-216">
         [215]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">
        Sports
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Sports">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wroclaw_Munincipal_Stadium_2019.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1894" data-file-width="3371" decoding="async" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Wroclaw_Munincipal_Stadium_2019.jpg/220px-Wroclaw_Munincipal_Stadium_2019.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Wroclaw_Munincipal_Stadium_2019.jpg/330px-Wroclaw_Munincipal_Stadium_2019.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Wroclaw_Munincipal_Stadium_2019.jpg/440px-Wroclaw_Munincipal_Stadium_2019.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wroclaw_Munincipal_Stadium_2019.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stadion_Miejski,_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Stadion Miejski, Wrocław">
          Municipal Stadium
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wroclaw_Olympic_Stadium_aerial_photograph_2017_P04.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2466" data-file-width="4384" decoding="async" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Wroclaw_Olympic_Stadium_aerial_photograph_2017_P04.jpg/220px-Wroclaw_Olympic_Stadium_aerial_photograph_2017_P04.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Wroclaw_Olympic_Stadium_aerial_photograph_2017_P04.jpg/330px-Wroclaw_Olympic_Stadium_aerial_photograph_2017_P04.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Wroclaw_Olympic_Stadium_aerial_photograph_2017_P04.jpg/440px-Wroclaw_Olympic_Stadium_aerial_photograph_2017_P04.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wroclaw_Olympic_Stadium_aerial_photograph_2017_P04.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Olympic_Stadium_(Wroc%C5%82aw)" title="Olympic Stadium (Wrocław)">
          Olympic Stadium
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The area of Wrocław is home to many popular
       <a href="/wiki/Professional_sports" title="Professional sports">
        professional sports
       </a>
       teams; the most popular sport is
       <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">
        football
       </a>
       (
       <a href="/wiki/%C5%9Al%C4%85sk_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Śląsk Wrocław">
        Śląsk Wrocław
       </a>
       club – Polish Champion in 1977 and 2012), followed by
       <a href="/wiki/Basketball" title="Basketball">
        basketball
       </a>
       (
       <a href="/wiki/%C5%9Al%C4%85sk_Wroc%C5%82aw_(basketball)" title="Śląsk Wrocław (basketball)">
        Śląsk Wrocław Basketball Club
       </a>
       – award-winning men's basketball team and 17-time Polish Champion).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-217">
        <a href="#cite_note-217">
         [216]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Matches of
       <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_Group_A" title="UEFA Euro 2012 Group A">
        Group A
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">
        UEFA Euro 2012
       </a>
       's were held at Wrocław at the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stadion_Miejski_(Wroc%C5%82aw)" title="Stadion Miejski (Wrocław)">
        Municipal Stadium
       </a>
       . Matches of
       <a href="/wiki/EuroBasket_1963" title="EuroBasket 1963">
        EuroBasket 1963
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/EuroBasket_2009" title="EuroBasket 2009">
        EuroBasket 2009
       </a>
       , as well as
       <a href="/wiki/2009_Women%27s_European_Volleyball_Championship" title="2009 Women's European Volleyball Championship">
        2009 Women's European Volleyball Championship
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/2014_FIVB_Volleyball_Men%27s_World_Championship" title="2014 FIVB Volleyball Men's World Championship">
        2014 FIVB Volleyball Men's World Championship
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/2016_European_Men%27s_Handball_Championship" title="2016 European Men's Handball Championship">
        2016 European Men's Handball Championship
       </a>
       were also held in Wrocław. Wrocław was the host of the
       <a href="/wiki/2013_World_Weightlifting_Championships" title="2013 World Weightlifting Championships">
        2013 World Weightlifting Championships
       </a>
       and will the host World Championship 2016 of
       <a href="/wiki/Duplicate_bridge" title="Duplicate bridge">
        Duplicate bridge
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/World_Games" title="World Games">
        World Games
       </a>
       2017, a competition in 37 non-Olympic sport disciplines.
      </p>
      <p>
       The
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Olympic_Stadium_(Wroc%C5%82aw)" title="Olympic Stadium (Wrocław)">
        Olympic Stadium
       </a>
       in Wrocław hosts the
       <a href="/wiki/Speedway_Grand_Prix_of_Poland" title="Speedway Grand Prix of Poland">
        Speedway Grand Prix of Poland
       </a>
       . It is also the home arena of the popular
       <a href="/wiki/Motorcycle_speedway" title="Motorcycle speedway">
        motorcycle speedway
       </a>
       club
       <a href="/wiki/WTS_Sparta_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="WTS Sparta Wrocław">
        WTS Sparta Wrocław
       </a>
       , four-time
       <a href="/wiki/Team_Speedway_Polish_Championship" title="Team Speedway Polish Championship">
        Polish Champion
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       A
       <a href="/wiki/Marathon" title="Marathon">
        marathon
       </a>
       takes place in Wrocław every year in September.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-218">
        <a href="#cite_note-218">
         [217]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Wrocław also hosts the
       <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw_Open" title="Wrocław Open">
        Wrocław Open
       </a>
       , a professional tennis tournament that is part of the
       <a href="/wiki/ATP_Challenger_Tour" title="ATP Challenger Tour">
        ATP Challenger Tour
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span id="Men.27s_sports">
       </span>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Men's_sports">
        Men's sports
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wroc%C5%82aw&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Men's sports">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/%C5%9Al%C4%85sk_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Śląsk Wrocław">
         Śląsk Wrocław
        </a>
        : men's
        <a href="/wiki/Football_in_Poland" title="Football in Poland">
         football
        </a>
        team,
        <a href="/wiki/List_of_Polish_football_champions" title="List of Polish football champions">
         Polish Championship in Football
        </a>
        1977, 2012;
        <a href="/wiki/Polish_Cup" title="Polish Cup">
         Polish Cup
        </a>
        winner 1976, 1987;
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Polish_SuperCup" title="Polish SuperCup">
         Polish SuperCup
        </a>
        winner 1987, 2012;
        <a href="/wiki/Ekstraklasa_Cup" title="Ekstraklasa Cup">
         Polish League Cup
        </a>
        winner 2009. Now in
        <a href="/wiki/Ekstraklasa" title="Ekstraklasa">
         Ekstraklasa
        </a>
        (Polish Premier League).
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/%C5%9Al%C4%85sk_Wroc%C5%82aw_(basketball)" title="Śląsk Wrocław (basketball)">
         Śląsk Wrocław
        </a>
        (previous names: BASCO Śląsk Wrocław, ASCO Śląsk Wrocław, Bergson Śląsk Wrocław, Era Śląsk Wrocław, Deichmann Śląsk Wrocław, Idea Śląsk Wrocław, Zepter Idea Śląsk Wrocław, Zepter Śląsk Wrocław, Śląsk ESKA Wrocław, PCS Śląsk Wrocław, WKS Śląsk Wrocław)—men's
        <a href="/wiki/Basketball" title="Basketball">
         basketball
        </a>
        team, 17 times Polish Champion, six times
        <a href="/wiki/Runner-up" title="Runner-up">
         runner-up
        </a>
        , 14 times third place; 12 times Polish Cup winner.
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/%C5%9Al%C4%85sk_Wroc%C5%82aw_(handball)" title="Śląsk Wrocław (handball)">
         Śląsk Wrocław
        </a>
        : men's
        <a href="/wiki/Handball_in_Poland" title="Handball in Poland">
         handball
        </a>
        team, 15-time Polish Champion.
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/WTS_Sparta_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="WTS Sparta Wrocław">
         WTS Sparta Wrocław
        </a>
        :
        <a href="/wiki/Motorcycle_speedway" title="Motorcycle speedway">
         motorcycle speedway
        </a>
        team, four-time Polish Champion.
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Gwardia_Wroc%C5%82aw_(men%27s_volleyball)" title="Gwardia Wrocław (men's volleyball)">
         Gwardia Wrocław
        </a>
        :
        <a href="/wiki/Volleyball_in_Poland" title="Volleyball in Poland">
         volleyball
        </a>
        team, three-time Polish Champion.
       </li>
       <li>
        KS Rugby Wrocław:
        <a href="/wiki/Rugby_union" title="Rugby union">
         rugby union
        </a>
        team.
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Panthers_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Panthers Wrocław">
         Panthers Wrocław
        </a>
        : American football team. Panthers joined
        <a href="/wiki/European_League_of_Football" title="European League of Football">
         European League of Football
        </a>
        (ELF) which is an 8-team professional league, the first league in Europe since the demise of
        <a href="/wiki/NFL_Europe" title="NFL Europe">
         NFL Europe
        </a>
        .
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-219">
         <a href="#cite_note-219">
          [218]
         </a>
        </sup>
        The Panthers will start playing games against teams from
        <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">
         Germany
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">
         Spain
        </a>
        in June 2021.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-220">
         <a href="#cite_note-220">
          [219]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h3>
       <span id="Women.27s_sports">
       </span>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Women's_sports">

       <span class="mw-editsection">

        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        WKS Śląsk Wrocław (formerly
        <a href="/wiki/K%C5%9A_AZS_Wroc%C5%82aw" title="KŚ AZS Wrocław">
         KŚ AZS Wrocław
        </a>
        ): women's
        <a href="/wiki/Football_in_Poland" title="Football in Poland">

        </a>
        team.
       </li>
       <li>

        </a>
        team.
       </li>
       <li>
        AZS AE Wrocław: women's

         table tennis
        </a>
        team.
       </li>

        </a>
        : women's

        </a>

       </li>
      </ul>

                     <td style="width:5em;">
                     </td>
                     <td class="navbox-list" style="padding:0px;text-align:left;;;;width:50%;">
                      <div>
                       <ul>
                        <li>
                         <b>
                          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/World_Games_1981" title="World Games 1981">
                           1981
                          </a>
                          :
                         </b>
                         <span class="flagicon">
                          <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">
                           <img alt="United States" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="650" data-file-width="1235" decoding="async" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" width="23"/>
